Guangdong Province

Issuing Treasury Bills

Total Amount of 2 Million Yuan

Guangzhou Correspondence. The Guangdong Provincial Government recently issued short-term financial treasury bills of the Republic of China, 23rd year, totaling 2 million yuan, with the provincial treasury's revenue from the provincial business tax and deed tax as collateral. The Guangdong Provincial Bank is responsible for soliciting subscriptions. From the date of issuance, the first month is the issuance period, and from the third month, the principal and interest are repaid in equal installments over three months. The order is determined by lottery. The lottery date is set on the last day of the third, fourth, and fifth months to repay the principal and interest. Guangdong Provincial Bank cash vouchers are designated for payment. The treasury bills are set at a monthly interest rate of one cent, that is, each silver hundred yuan yields three yuan in interest. Starting from the first day of the third month after issuance, the Finance Department will allocate 25,000 yuan daily from the business tax and deed tax revenue until the end of the month, allocating the full amount of principal and interest due for that month. The treasury bills are divided into four types: 100 yuan, 50 yuan, 10 yuan, and 5 yuan. However, part of the 5 yuan bills are divided into five parts in order to distribute odd amounts. It is decided to issue them on September 10. The treasury bills are in bearer form. All commercial banks, silver shops, and miscellaneous shops may distribute them in accordance with the regulations. The current issuance will collect funds at a 98% discount to the face value. When repaying the principal and interest in the future, the Provincial Bank will pay with silver dollars converted from the provincial vouchers allocated by the Finance Department. During the issuance period, underwriters of treasury bills with a face value of more than 1,000 yuan will be specially authorized by the Provincial Bank to be treated as distributors, paying funds and receiving vouchers at a 93% discount. The distribution period for treasury bills is from September 10 to October 9. Yesterday, the Provincial Bank officially announced the issuance regulations and distribution methods to all sectors. (9th)

New Life Movement Association

Intensifying Efforts

Nanchang Correspondence. Since its reorganization and establishment, the Nanchang New Life Movement Association has moved from verbal or active propaganda to practical and concrete implementation. Due to the enthusiasm and perseverance of the organizers, this implementation has recently achieved remarkable results in various aspects of Nanchang. Therefore, the work is becoming increasingly tense, and people from all walks of life who come here to visit are also constantly coming. Yesterday, the reporter interviewed the local New Life Movement authorities and learned about the various situations in great detail, and specially recorded them in detail as follows:

The Nanchang New Life Movement implementation work is based on the idea of ​​starting near and moving far, focusing on Nanchang City and the Nansun Road areas. It first starts with the "order" and "cleanliness" movements in organizations, groups, public places, and transportation arteries, and then extends to families and individuals. The methods are divided into three types: persuasion, inspection, and competition. The scope of implementation in Nanchang City includes streets, train stations, wharves, theaters, parks, schools, public offices, people's organizations, factories, hotels, restaurants, bathhouses, barbershops, and other stores. On Nansun Road, it includes train stations, trains, ferries, and wharves. For the convenience of work, various methods such as division by district, industry, category, and period are adopted. At the same time, the military police are requested to provide assistance. Since the start of the work, various organizations have been actively launched: (1) Youth Holiday Service Corps. This corps was originally organized by the Education Department and later transferred to the jurisdiction of the association. During the holidays, young students in the province are divided into districts and groups to provide services. The city is divided into ten districts, with more than 200 groups, and three directly affiliated teams. The heads of each district are the principals of each school, and the captains of the directly affiliated teams are also appointed by the association. Each district group is assigned a section by the association and provides services on a daily and punctual basis under the leadership of the group leader. The first directly affiliated team regularly provides services on Nansun Road. The second directly affiliated team selects young people from various schools to specialize in serving important transportation areas such as train stations and wharves. The third directly affiliated team consists of students from the Special Education Teacher Training Institute and serves in hotels, restaurants, and various public entertainment venues. (2) Store Service Personnel. Each store designates one person as a service person, who, in addition to serving inside the store, also pays attention to the hygiene and order of the sidewalk, road, or street in front of the store. After the association convened the executive and supervisory committees of the Nanchang City Chamber of Commerce and the responsible persons of various trade associations three times, all the detailed measures were completely decided. On the one hand, the service regulations were passed, and on the other hand, the association created the style of armband and distributed them to each service person to wear for service, and explained the various misunderstandings from the outside, such as saying that the service person is a soldier, will be negligent in his own business in the future, and has no respect for the shop owner, etc. Now, each industry has complied with the regulations and enthusiastically reported the names of the service personnel to the association. In the future, each of the more than 9,000 stores in the city will have a New Life Movement cell, and the performance of its results will be considerable. (3) Service Personnel of Various Agencies. The heads of each agency select a number of employees who are enthusiastic about the New Life Movement to serve as service personnel. In addition to serving in each agency, they are also responsible for promoting a new life at home for their colleagues. (4) Women's Service Corps. Organized by employed intellectual women to guide family improvement and assist in rescuing women and children. (5) Amateur Service Corps. All freelance professionals voluntarily participate in the service in their spare time and are organized by the association to serve on streets, wharves, train stations, and vegetable markets. The above three, four, and five types of organizations are currently being actively launched, so that they can be realized step by step. Now, most primary and secondary schools in the city have started classes. The association has changed the Youth Service Corps into a permanent organization and decided on five principles: 1. Continue to implement training; 2. Expand the number of members; 3. Strictly organize the service corps; 4. Change its scope of service; 5. Shorten its service time. This was decided at the joint meeting of the heads of each district and the captains of the directly affiliated teams convened in recent days. In addition, the association has decided on various aspects of the implementation work within this month, including: 1. Completing 200 to 1,000 standard families and holding a public exhibition; 2. Promoting a new life in factories; 3. Expanding the organization of various members and providing training; 4. A combined general mobilization and regular general inspection; 5. Holding a new life competition among various service team members, various agencies, groups, schools, stores, and public places to thoroughly check past work and promote future work. In short, the atmosphere in all aspects is very active and tense, full of vigor, and there is enough for other places to emulate. (September 13)

Ringleader Luo Binghui Injured in Qingyuan Battle

Nanchang Correspondence. Military news. According to captured bandits, the recent intrusion into Qingyuan was carried out by the troops of the pseudo-Seventh Army Corps Commander Luo Binghui, a total of three regiments, with more than 1,000 people in each regiment, totaling more than 2,000 guns and more than 40 light machine guns. They captured the forward position of Zhukou in Rixiang and engaged in fierce fighting with the Zhejiang Security Regiment. The bandits suffered more than 800 casualties, with two battalion commanders and seven company commanders killed. The pseudo-corps commander was shot in the right forearm and was carried away on a stretcher with the army. The bandit Luo is less than five feet tall and has a thin appearance. It is said that the bandits suffered heavy losses in this battle.

Also, news. Refugees who escaped from the Jiangkou area said that after the National Army's various routes of suppression, the bandits have become turtles in a jar. Now, the bandits are coercing elderly men and women to organize the Red Guards, hoping to make a final struggle and prolong their lives. In the Jiangkou area, because there are no able-bodied men to draw, elderly men and women between the ages of 40 and 60 are coerced to form the Red Guards, and now 500 to 600 people have been assigned to be driven by the Red bandits. The Jiangkou Pseudo-Trade Bureau still exists, with the pseudo-director being Li Hongqiu, and the bureau address is located in the Guangyu Feng store there. The Jiangkou Pseudo-District Government is located at the Jiangkou Wharf, and the pseudo-chairman is Lai. The bandits in Xingguo Gaoxing Market recently resisted the National Army for three or four days. The bandits suffered a miserable defeat, with corpses piled up. The bandit corpses near Gaoxing Market were exposed, and the stench traveled for several miles. The National Army is now building fortresses in the Libu section, handling village clearance, and sending teams to advance on guerrillas, and so on. (September 15)

Songjiang

The Defense Force Will Be Reorganized Again

After the county defense force was reorganized into two platoons with two squads, the self-defense corps in Fengjing, Tinglin, Tianmashan, Sijing, Xinzhuang and other places were also reorganized into squads. The salaries were still collected and supplied by local communities to protect the area. Except for the squad in Fengjing, which has been disbanded, all the defense forces in Tinglin and other four places have been reorganized into two squads and maintained as before. Now, it is learned that the Provincial Security Department has sent news of a comprehensive reorganization. The original First Platoon in the county has an insufficient number of people. It is planned to use the Second Platoon as the First Platoon and the original First Platoon as the Second Platoon. However, the Provincial Government believes that the local donations for the squads in Tinglin and other places are inappropriate and has sent news of their abolition. Therefore, the general captain Shen Bangda went to the province and personally visited Director Xiang of the Security Department, stating that the four major towns in the county had all been robbed by bandits in the past. Local communities are happy to contribute to the defense force to suppress the area, and requested permission to maintain the status quo. It is heard that Director Xiang ordered Captain Shen to return to Songjiang, convene representatives from various places to hold a meeting, discuss whether the squads in various places should exist, and the issue of salaries, etc., and submit it to the Provincial Government for approval before they can be maintained. Therefore, Captain Shen plans to convene local figures to discuss before the reorganization.

Jiashan

Luxingbang Robbery Injures People

Last night at midnight, five or six bandits suddenly came to the Luxingbang area of Yuyao, speaking in mixed accents, carrying electric torches and quick-firing weapons. They opened the gate of the house of Jin Huisheng, a farmer from Shaoxing, and warned him not to make any noise. They overturned boxes and cabinets and carried out a rampant robbery. A farmhand, Wang, took the opportunity to report to the Zhenjiang police regiment, but was spotted by a bandit guarding the room, who grabbed him and beat him severely, causing serious injuries. After the bandits obtained the loot, they fled eastward.

Rice Shop Partner Drowns Himself

Pan Xuesun from Yuyao was a partner in the Xietai Hing rice shop in Zhujing. In the autumn of last year, he suddenly suffered from anal malaria. After a hundred ways of treatment, he finally recovered a little. Therefore, he was absent from work for half a year. When he came to the store this spring, his body had not yet recovered, and he was lazy to work. The shop owner was quite annoyed with Pan, but Pan was always depressed. In addition, his anal malaria recurred, and he was economically strapped and unable to seek further treatment. Therefore, on the night of the 13th, he secretly went to the wooden raft and jumped into the clear stream to commit suicide.

Suzhou

National Goods Commercial Center Postpones Opening

The Suzhou National Goods Commercial Center, initiated and founded by Shi Junqing, chairman of the Suzhou Chamber of Commerce, raised more than 200,000 yuan and built a three-story building in the Beiju area, which is about to be completed. It was originally scheduled to open on the first day of the national calendar. However, due to the unresolved issue of renting stores, the opening on the first day of the national calendar is impossible. It may be postponed to the first day of the lunar calendar. The building has more than 500 rooms. Stores are opened on the first and second floors, and the remaining rooms are used to open a national goods paradise. However, the paradise is not run by the company, but is also open to merchants. It is currently in negotiations.

The Corruption Case of the Farmland Tax Is Resolved Vaguely

The Wuxian Farmland Tax Corruption Case, which has attracted attention from all sides, was investigated secretly by Dong Binqian, dispatched by the Finance Department. The case is generally clear. There are indeed problems with the privately collected and farmer-owed parts. However, the fault of the private collection does not lie with the director of the farmland tax, but with the registrar's office and the various map makers who colluded to commit fraud. Therefore, the registrar's office manager Qian Zhonghua was taken into custody. In the part owed by the farmers, it was found that Feng Sisushang owed thousands of gold in grain over the years. As for the part of wasteland reclamation, whether there are any corrupt practices, because there are more than 1,000 books of records, it is particularly difficult to check. If you want to thoroughly investigate, it will take more than three or four months. Committee member Dong believes that the private collection involves hundreds of people. Investigating each one will require a major prison sentence. Therefore, he left Suzhou a few days ago to report to Director Zhao of the Finance Department and ask for instructions. Director Zhao immediately summoned the Wuxian County Chief to the province the day before yesterday to discuss countermeasures together. Now the Wuxian County Chief has returned to Suzhou, and Committee member Dong must also come to Suzhou today or tomorrow to handle the conclusion matters. According to rumors, in addition to punishing Qian Zhonghua, others will not be pursued, and it will be resolved vaguely.

Wuxi

Smoking Without a License Will Be Dealt With by Military Law

The County Anti-Smoking Committee has drawn lots to determine the location of opium dens and sales points in urban and rural areas. In recent days, the County Committee has ordered its subordinates to seriously handle the guarantee matters. Yesterday, the committee held another ad hoc meeting and decided: (1) According to the instructions of the Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee, each district should set up one opium den. However, in districts with a large number of smokers, it seems insufficient to supply the demand. It is allowed to make changes and add more, with two additional dens in the first district, one in the third district, and one in the eighth district. (2) Committee member Cheng was elected to verify the signing, and committee members Qian, Li, and Chen drew lots, Secretary Yao recorded the books, and Section Chief Hua counted the signs. The lottery results were: Ding Chanming "Yuanji" and Lian Tang "Yonglong" in the first district, Zhu Yuan "Youli" in the third district, and Qian Yingzhang "Dada" in the eighth district. (3) The County Committee originally planned to have one opium den in the urban area. Now, after adding two more, there are a total of three. The committee also drew lots to determine the location of each den. The location is in the city center, with Ding Chanming in Nanmen and Lian Tang outside Guangfumen. At the same time, the committee felt deeply sorry that the registration of smokers in the county was still waiting and seeing, hoping to hide. Yesterday, it specially listed the following articles as a final warning: (1) Those who are addicted but have not registered or reported their intention to quit will be immediately detained and forced to register. (2) After the registration period expires at the end of September, there will be absolutely no extension. From October 1, smoking without a license will be dealt with by military law. (3) Those who report smoking without a license and are found to be true will be rewarded with a bonus of up to 100 yuan. The bonus will be borne by the smoker. However, those who make false accusations will be punished in reverse according to military law. (4) Those who do not want to register and obtain a license to smoke again must report to quit. Those who quit on their own must also register their names. Otherwise, once discovered, it will be difficult to distinguish between jade and stone, and the stakes are huge. (5) Those who have not applied for registration in the surveyed areas must quickly go to the committee in the urban area to apply for registration. Those who are willing to register in advance in the unsurveyed areas can also go to the committee to apply for registration in advance to avoid missing the opportunity. (6) If people who are not laborers or poor people fraudulently obtain a Class B license, they must still exchange it for a license and pay the fee. (7) The smoking cessation license is only for the personal use of the holder and may not be shared by a household or lent to others. In particular, the license may not be used to lure or protect others to smoke. If there is any violation, in addition to canceling the holder's registration, it will be dealt with according to military law.

Changzhou

Bandit Leader Ren Haoming Escorted to Changzhou

Bandit leader Ren Haoming of Wuyi County has committed numerous crimes and has been wanted. The bandit was hiding in Shanghai and has not been captured. However, he was recently arrested in Shanghai for another case and sent to the First Special District Court. The Wujin County Government heard the news and immediately sent personnel to escort him back. However, due to issues such as procedures and documents, the escort to Changzhou was delayed. The county government received an official letter from the First Special District Court of Shanghai the day before yesterday, requesting to send personnel to escort him back. It immediately sent Detective Captain Ni Gusheng, detective Hu Shaoqing, and four security team members to Shanghai on the 15th. After submitting the official documents to the Special Court, the court handed the bandit Ren over to Captain Ni to take back. They then boarded the express train at 1:06 pm and escorted him to Changzhou. When they left Shanghai, they were escorted by detectives from the Chinese and French Concessions. When the train arrived at Changzhou Station, the entire detective team was present at the station to take care of it, in order to prevent accidents.

The county's various legal groups, because the Jinan Seven Companies were ordered by the Lianghuai Transportation Envoy to move north, which concerns the commercial safety of Yangcheng, organized a Joint Association for Maintaining the Salt Industry to discuss countermeasures. On one hand, the county party headquarters, led by the Party Secretary, sent a telegram to Transportation Envoy Miao, requesting him to withdraw the order. It is learned that the county party headquarters received a reply from Miao yesterday, which stated that the telegram had been read. After investigating the previous order from the Ministry of Finance, the seven companies in Jinan should focus on salt production, and the center of gravity should be in Yuxia. However, the center of gravity for issuing orders by the seven companies is still in Yangzhou, which has caused a lack of coordination in the matters that should be promoted and reformed in Yuxia. This is detrimental to the future of rectification and should be promptly advised to quickly shift the center of gravity in order to be able to handle matters under the official government at any time and increase efficiency. It has been repeatedly ordered to comply with the record. This time, the time limit was set for the seven companies to move the headquarters to Banpu or Chenjiagang, which was originally to execute the Ministry's order. I don't know what the so-called destruction of established rules in the telegram refers to. The matter concerns the order of the Ministry, so there is no need to discuss the request to withdraw the order. I hope to explain to all sectors that they must not obstruct important government affairs. If incidents occur as a result, all responsibilities shall be borne by the various legal groups, and so on. The county party headquarters received the telegram and immediately notified the Maintenance Association and various legal groups. The association has scheduled the third executive committee meeting to be held at the county party headquarters at 5:00 pm today (16th). All executives have been notified and are expected to attend. Also, since receiving the northern migration order, the Dayuan Company has been actively preparing for several days. Because Banpu is close to the Transportation Office, but the transportation is quite inconvenient, it has established a Pu branch in Xinpu and hired Fang Hanzhang, the secretary of the Transportation Office, as the manager. Although the name of the Yangzhou headquarters still exists, it has actually become a liaison office. This is used to ease the atmosphere in Yangzhou. The other six companies will also follow suit in order.

Mantingfang

Private Receipt of Stolen Goods Case

Case: Fu Rong Privately Received 300 Dozen Rasps

The Thief Has Been Punished, Qin Is Also Being Prosecuted

The Mantingfang area on Wuma Road has always been known for receiving stolen goods for profit. Qin Furong also opened Qin Fuxing Hardware Store in the area, building his business by receiving stolen goods and accumulating tens of thousands of gold, yet he did not cease his activities. In August of this year, Zhang Binggen, a native of Yuyao and employee of De Taicheng Hardware Store at No. 181 Henan Road, stole 600 dozen rasps from the store, worth three to four thousand yuan. Three hundred dozen of these stolen goods were directly sold cheaply to Qin Fuxing at a price of three yuan per dozen. After some time, Yu Wenbiao, the assistant manager of De Taicheng Store, found out and reported it to the police. Zhang Binggen was arrested and sent to the criminal court of the First Special District Court. After interrogation, he was sentenced to three months in prison. The detectives investigated the stolen goods at Qin's place. Qin claimed that Zhang had peddled 20 dozen, but 10 dozen had already been sold. Therefore, the court was requested to issue a summons. The case was heard yesterday morning by Judge Deng Baosen of the Second Criminal Court. Qin Furong hired lawyer Fan Gang to represent him. First, lawyer Qian Xunjiu, representing the police, stated the facts of the case and prosecuted him for receiving stolen goods. Then, Zhang Binggen was brought from the Western Prison for questioning. According to his confession, he had stolen and sold 300 dozen rasps to Qin Furong from April to August, at a price of three yuan per dozen. Next, Yu Jiaobiao testified that the rasps were exclusively sold by their store and had a secret mark. The purchase price was over six yuan per dozen, and the defendant Qin Furong had come to the store to buy them in bulk. Lawyer E Sen was also hired, claiming compensation for the losses, which should be calculated based on 300 dozen. When questioned, Qin Furong's testimony was evasive. Judge Deng ruled that further investigation was necessary and ordered a rescheduling for further verification on the morning of the 18th.

Lin Shaozhang's Bigamy Case

Appeal After Sentencing

The Third Branch of the High Court Held a Trial the Day Before Yesterday

The Case Still Requires Investigation

Lin Shaozhang, a Ningbo native residing at No. 35 Hongfuli, Dengtu Road, Public Concession, is 46 years old this year. He has been diligently engaged in business over the years and has accumulated some wealth. He had only one son, named Weixian, who unfortunately died of illness in the early summer of last year. Because of his eagerness to have a son, he disliked his wife Zhang's old age and inability to bear children. Therefore, in early July of this year, through a matchmaker, he married Zhao Shuiying, a Suzhou woman (21 years old this year), as a concubine. Initially, the matchmakers concealed the truth from Zhao, saying it was a "round string." Then, a formal wedding ceremony was held at No. 26 Yongchengli, Xujiahui Road, French Concession. After living together for a short time, they moved around. Lin, in order to save expenses, moved Zhao to No. 36 Hongfuli, next door to his own residence. Unexpectedly, Lin's wife Zhang became jealous and often went to Zhao's place to make trouble and quarrel. Zhao then learned that Lin still had a wife. Lin, unable to bear his wife's harassment, stopped visiting his concubine, and ignored Zhao's daily necessities. Zhao, at this point, believed that Lin had committed bigamy and abandonment. Since Lin's marriage and crime took place in the French Concession, Zhao reported it to the French police on June 26th of this year. The police dispatched detectives to cooperate with the Public Concession police to arrest Lin and bring him to the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer filed a public prosecution against Lin for bigamy. After summoning the matchmakers and witnesses to court, the trial concluded, and Lin Shaozhang was found guilty of bigamy and sentenced to four months of imprisonment. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that Lin did not accept the judgment and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court accepted the appeal and, the day before yesterday, Chief Judge Guo, with the assistance of Judges Sun and Fan, Prosecutor Zhang, specially convened a collegial panel for trial. Because the case still required investigation, the court ordered a postponement for further questioning.

Gaoqiao

Rural Improvement Association Tea Party Record

The Shanghai Gaoqiao Rural Improvement Association held a tea party at 9:00 AM on the 15th at the local Fire Brigade, inviting local elders and leaders from all walks of life. It was a heavy rain, but the number of participants did not decrease as a result. Attendees included Ding Fengshan, Ding Rusong, Zhong Yuliang, Zhan Chun, Lan Zhusan, Lai Douyan, Huang Zhicheng, Chen Yuru, Xu Bingzhang, Cai Zhiyuan, and others, totaling 27 people. After ringing the bell, the meeting began as scheduled. First, Chairman Du Yuesheng delegated Wang Kuiying to report, saying: "Elders, leaders, Chairman Du Yuesheng was originally going to personally preside over everything at today's reception, but due to being busy, he had to notify me to temporarily represent him and say a few words. Regarding the initiation and preparation, internal organization, and work plan of the Gaoqiao Rural Improvement Association, there are printed materials here, and everyone can take a copy to read. There is no need for me to elaborate. Today, I want to say a few words that are not in the printed materials. That is, why does Chairman Du Yuesheng spend money and effort to initiate and organize this association? Why do my colleagues and I, and all the interns, come here to do rural improvement work? The first reason for Chairman Du Yuesheng's initiation and organization is the most obvious, because this is his hometown. Patriotism must start with loving the hometown. The second reason is that China is founded on agriculture, and in the past one or two years, rural bankruptcy and continuous disasters have affected the sluggishness of the city, causing various construction projects in politics, economy, and culture to stagnate invisibly. If we don't start with the countryside, we can't talk about so-called production and construction. The third reason is that Chairman Du Yuesheng deeply believes that the people of Gaoqiao have always been enthusiastic about public welfare and have achieved good results in the past. Public security, hygiene, and education have also made great progress. With the Improvement Association here, we will surely receive the assistance and guidance of all elders and leaders. I hope that in a few years, Gaoqiao can become a model autonomous region, so that nearby places and all parts of the country can hear the news and imitate it, forming the backbone force for building China, so that we can gradually realize the highest ideal of the Prime Minister's Three Principles of the People. As for my colleagues and others coming here to work, on the one hand, we are carrying out the purpose of Chairman Du and all the directors and members, and strive to express and implement it. On the other hand, it is also providing us young people with a place to practice patriotism and love for the people. Because my colleagues and others feel that the biggest crisis in our country at present is not only the aggression of the great powers and the disturbance of the Communist Party, but also that the general youth have abandoned their basic organization of rural society and are all running to the bustling places of big cities. As a result, cash and all great construction are concentrated in big cities, suffering from a bloated belly, unable to digest, cultivating speculative psychology, extravagant life, and creating all kinds of unimaginable evils. As a result, it is still a perverted and deformed development. According to our experience and belief, unless there are a group of passionate young people, full of the spirit of sacrifice, service, adventure, and struggle, and strive to create a new atmosphere, so that the outstanding young people in the country all take improving rural life as their duty, and they can also develop their personal ambitions without throwing themselves into the bustling cities. Gradually, the idle capital of the cities will slowly be transferred back to the countryside. Not only will the income of farmers increase and their lives become prosperous, but also education, industry, commerce, social undertakings, and political facilities can be universally developed in the countryside. After ten years of accumulating wealth and ten years of education, we can talk about building the country, resisting foreign aggression, and reviving the nation. Although the elders present may not be able to see such a grand occasion, we adults and young people may not necessarily be able to see it in our lifetime. But as the saying goes, "The predecessors planted the trees, and the descendants enjoy the shade." As long as we adhere to the spirit of Jingwei filling the sea and the Old Man moving the mountain, our children and grandchildren will definitely continue our cause, so that our Chinese nation will regain the glory in history. Although our scope of work in Gaoqiao is small, its impact is very large. The colleagues of the office hold a humble attitude of learning and a spirit of dedication to service, and are willing to follow the elders and leaders from all walks of life and strive to accomplish this great undertaking." Next, the cadres and staff were introduced, and Mr. Liu Guofan, a cadre of the Rural Education Department, was invited to speak, saying: "I am from Liaoning in Northeast China, and I have personally tasted the suffering of national subjugation. However, Japanese imperialism is ambitious and wants to annex China every day. Looking back, the reasons why we cannot resist foreign aggression are four: ignorance, weakness, poverty, and selfishness. I think that the way out for China should start from the basic level and thoroughly eradicate the above root causes, that is, improve education, increase productivity, pay attention to personality cultivation, and train unity and cooperation." Finally, he said, "My colleagues and I are weak in ability, and I hope that the local elders and leaders from all walks of life will cooperate and assist." Next, Mr. Zhan Chun, the branch director of the Public Security Bureau, spoke, saying: "The Gaoqiao Rural Improvement Association takes improving the countryside as its duty. If the rural improvement is successful, there will be solutions in economic, educational, and political aspects. The future of the country and the nation can be opened up. China is a whole, so various undertakings should not be divided and demarcated, but should be done with one heart and one mind. If Gaoqiao succeeds, all parts of the country will respond to the news, which will not only benefit one place in Gaoqiao, but also be a blessing to the whole country. If the Public Security Bureau needs help during the rural survey, please notify us by letter, and I will send people to protect it to facilitate the process." Next, Mr. Zhong Yuliang spoke, mainly saying: "Welcome the personnel of the Rural Improvement Association office. At the same time, I feel that the planned plans and steps are very appropriate. Among them, such as the migrant workers' training institute and the public cemetery, are essential things in Gaoqiao. I deeply hope that the gentlemen in the office and the local elders will cooperate and carry them out together." Next, Mr. Lai Douyan spoke, mainly saying: "There are many difficulties in handling health administration, and the economic life of farmers is the most important. Secondly, a career cannot be successful alone. Now that we have comrades, I hope to cooperate, then not only will health be a solution, but other aspects will also be a solution." Next, Mr. Ding Fengshan spoke, mainly saying: "The population of Gaoqiao is not very accurate, especially the farmers in the smaller villages have not yet developed the habit of reporting deaths and marriages, and they often conceal them. Therefore, some bad elements can lurk unnoticed. In the past three months, more than 20 households have been stolen, which hinders public security and cannot be ignored. I intend to organize farmers to implement the Baojia system and select fair people from the local area to serve as village chiefs, preferably with 100 households as a unit, with one person responsible for reporting births and deaths, then bad elements cannot stand and local public security will naturally be peaceful." After the tea party, Mr. Wang Kuiying, the chief director, expressed his thanks and said that in order to solicit opinions, a suggestion box was specially set up, and he asked the elders and leaders from all walks of life to continue to criticize and correct. It was almost 12 o'clock when the meeting was adjourned.

Strange Events in Heavy Rain

Snake's Head as Big as a Teacup

Countless Small Holes in the Tree Trunk

Gray Snake Falls from the Sky

The night before last, the city suddenly had a heavy thunderstorm. At around 8:00 PM, a thunderclap was suddenly heard at the intersection of Dongjie College Street, Dadongmen, Shanghai. A large snake fell from mid-air, its body gray, its head the size of a teacup, and its body about six feet long. A crowd of onlookers gathered for a time. When it fell, the snake's eyes were bright and it could still swim. Later, it was beaten to death by passers-by with iron hoes. The snake's body was burned with fire. It is said that it was thrown into the Huangpu River.

Ancient Tree Struck into Three Sections

At 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, the sky was covered with dark clouds and heavy rain poured down. Suddenly, a thunderclap was heard, shaking far and wide. A ball of lightning suddenly fell from the sky, striking an ancient tree on the north side of the Wangjiazhai Stone Bridge on Pusengtang Bridge Road into three sections. The tree fell to the west side of the road, and its last section was pulled up from the ground at the root. Upon closer inspection of the broken part of the tree trunk, countless small holes were found. At that time, nearby residents came to watch. According to someone in the audience, when the big tree fell, they caught a glimpse of a gecko about a foot long jumping out, and then they didn't know where it went. According to the elders there, the tree grew during the Ming Dynasty and has a history of more than 300 years. It is found that the tree has two hugs in circumference, half alive and half dead. There are houses on the east, south, and north sides of the tree. The villagers are amazed that it happened to fall to the west and did not collapse houses or injure people.

Page 13

Qianji Hotel

A Young Man Was Assassinated Last Night

Claiming to Be Xiong Guohua, He Did Not Go Out All Day Yesterday

Two Thugs Suddenly Arrived and Opened Fire Upon Seeing Him

—All Three Shots Hit Vital Points, Life in Danger—

Young Traveler

At 11:35 last night, a traveler at Qianji Hotel in Huajinli, Sima Road, was suddenly shot. Details are recorded below. Shenji Qianji Hotel at No. 37 Huajinli, Sima Road, received a young traveler wearing a dark gray serge long gown, a felt hat, and leather shoes at around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday (the 15th). He booked Room 34 on the second floor, next to the staircase entrance, at a daily rate of nine dimes and five cents.

Did Not Go Out All Day

Because the hotel saw that the young man was carrying a large suitcase, they did not ask him to pay the room fee in advance. The young man signed his name as Xiong Guohua, 34 years old, from Taizhou, Zhejiang, engaged in the electrical business. He went out once that night and returned to the hotel late at night. After reading various newspapers, he went to sleep. He did not go out all day yesterday.

Sudden Arrival of Thugs

At 11:00 last night, the young man ordered a bowl of shredded pork soup noodles from the waiter. After eating, he read the newspaper again. After the waiter brewed tea and sent it to the room, the young man closed the door and went to bed. Unexpectedly, less than half an hour later, at around 11:30, two thugs wearing black short clothes suddenly came downstairs. They went straight upstairs, reached out and knocked on the door of Room 34, and frequently called out Xiong Guohua's name.

—Three Shots Fired in Succession

Upon hearing the sound, Xiong got out of bed and opened the door. Upon seeing the two men, he did not recognize them. Just as he was about to ask, one of the two thugs suddenly pulled out a gun and fired three shots at Xiong in succession. Because they were so close, all the shots hit. Seeing that their purpose had been achieved, the thugs fled down the stairs in a panic, escaping without a trace.

Only a Glimmer of Life

After Xiong was shot and fell to the ground, blood flowed straight out. At the same time, the hotel waiters all rushed over. But Xiong, except for calling out "Waiter, hurry up," fell to the ground unconscious. The accounting room urgently reported to the police by telephone. The police chief immediately sent Chinese and Western detectives to the scene. After carefully examining the three shots that Xiong was hit by, one was in the mouth, one was in the left neck, and one was in the right chest, they immediately called an ambulance to send Xiong to Renji Hospital, but he only had a glimmer of life left.

Police Investigation

After the police inspected the scene, they brought Xiong's suitcase and the waiter on duty into the police station for investigation. Three shell casings were sent to the gun inspection room for examination. It is not yet known why Xiong was assassinated. The police have already begun to investigate Xiong Guohua's real name and whereabouts in order to arrest the murderer.

Verification of Double Suicide by Male and Female

In Room 520 of a certain hotel on Shanxi Road, there were two young male and female travelers, the man named Tong Jiaju and the woman named Zhao. The day before yesterday, they suddenly had a pessimistic thought and committed suicide by taking a large amount of Lysol and opium. Later, the hotel waiter Zhao Bingquan discovered it and sent the two men and women to Renji Hospital for treatment to no avail. They died one after another. The hospital reported to the General Patrol Room, and the patrolman ordered an investigation. The two bodies were sent to the Forensic Examination Office on Feilun Road for verification. It has been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday, a report was submitted to the First Special District Court, which appointed Prosecutor Tang to visit the office and verify that the bodies were real. It was then determined that the deceased Tong Jiaju, male, and Zhao, female, both died of poisoning before their deaths. In addition to the deceased's belongings temporarily stored in the police station for collection, the bodies were handed over to the Pushan Villa for collection.

Two Groups on Aidoa Road Re-petition

Banning Prostitutes from Standing Around and Causing Disturbances

The Fourteenth Branch of the First Special District Citizens' Association and the Aidoa Road Business Community Association, previously, due to the fact that prostitutes (commonly known as "wild chickens") on Zhengjia Wood Bridge, Dongxin Bridge, and Xizang Road on that road would stand in front of stores as soon as the lights came on at night, pulling people hard, causing passers-by to be afraid of them, resulting in customers of various stores not coming and avoiding them, causing business losses. The association had previously sent a letter to the Public Works Bureau requesting a ban. As a result, the prostitutes on various roads disappeared for several days, not daring to stand out to solicit customers until late at night. Unexpectedly, recently, the police have been a little negligent in catching them, and a group of prostitutes has relapsed, standing as before, pulling and dragging hard, and rampant as before. The letter stated, "Respectfully, the rampant situation of prostitutes on Aidoa Road, Zhengjia Wood Bridge, and Xizang Road was described in detail to your bureau by our association on September 1st, requesting a ban. We were pleased to have received instructions to handle the matter. Our association and various stores are deeply grateful and celebrating that we can get rid of the stains from now on in order to maintain the business in the store. Unexpectedly, the fact is very different. Since the 14th of this month, prostitutes have been standing on the street and pulling hard, just like before, no less than before. If they are caught, they will hide, and if they are not caught, they will not avoid it. This is not a proper solution. Your bureau should pay more attention and investigate the points mentioned in the previous letter. Strictly order the brothels to move to secluded places to remove the roots. At the very least, they should be prohibited from standing in front of stores. Otherwise, please send several plainclothes officers to patrol and arrest them every night to eliminate the traces of prostitutes, maintain commerce, and reassure customers. This is addressed to the Bureau of Public Works' Director Zhong."

Japanese Control of the Puppet Manchukuo Economy 6

Respectfully,

The complete Japanese control of the puppet Manchukuo economy has been advocated for two or three years. The reasons for its lack of implementation can be attributed to two main factors. First, internal conflicts within Japan itself have not been resolved. For instance, the diplomatic, colonial, and military departments stand in a three-legged opposition, or in other words, there are many divisions between financial cliques, bureaucrats, and warlords, hindering smooth progress. Second, international restrictions and China's resistance pose considerable constraints, forcing Japan to exercise some caution. Currently, the disharmony among Japan's own financial cliques, bureaucrats, and warlords is gradually decreasing. The so-called unified rule of "two in one" has become a possibility. The political impasse is expected to be broken, and efforts are being made to ease international tensions, hence the move towards economic control.

Before Japan implemented control over the "Manchukuo" economy, there was a minor event: the collection of iron scraps and purchase of iron-making raw materials. This matter may seem insignificant on the surface, but upon closer examination, we realize it holds profound implications. Although Japan proclaims to its citizens that it is self-sufficient in steel and iron, with domestic production reaching nearly 2.3 million tons, the reality is that the majority of steel and iron raw materials rely on external supply from places like the Malay Peninsula. During normal times, this does not pose a major problem. However, in times of war, there is a risk of supply being cut off. During this critical period, Japan is vigorously expanding its military industry, and the demand for steel and iron is naturally very high. Does this collection of steel and iron raw materials not contain far-reaching significance? Looking at this one small aspect of Japan's control of the puppet Manchukuo economy, one can understand its future direction. In terms of the mainland, the most sharply opposed in terms of economic interests and closely bordering the three northeastern provinces is the Soviet Union. The ideological influence exerted by the Soviet Union on Japanese society has made Japan feel very uneasy, yet it cannot be completely eradicated. Moreover, historical animosity exists, so the Japanese army has to maintain strict vigilance against the Soviet Union. In its first Five-Year Plan, the Soviet Union fully focused on the defense of the Far East, and now its military facilities are even more advanced. Its diplomatic skills are also very astute. After successfully joining the League of Nations, it has gained an advantageous position in the international arena. Despite loudly proclaiming its opposition to the Soviet Union, Japan is hesitant to take action. In this reluctance to act rashly, it has adopted this first step of controlling the puppet Manchukuo economy. The actual benefits gained from this control policy outweigh the losses, compared to advancing into Siberia.

This reminds us of the summer of the 20th year of the Republic (1931), when Japan appointed Yasuya Uchida, who was fluent in Russian, as president of the South Manchuria Railway, and named Isei Tatekawa, a former army officer and politician, as Governor-General of Korea, tasking them with planning the September 18th Incident, seizing the three northeastern provinces, and dealing with the Soviet Union. Unfortunately, we did not foresee this at the time, resulting in complete passivity and being manipulated by others. Now, Japan's so-called continental policy is still unforgettable. After the puppet Manchukuo's reorganization, its control over the "Manchukuo" economy, although containing anti-Soviet implications, is by no means limited to solely targeting the Soviet Union. This is what we must clearly understand today.

"I do not want to call General Johnson a liar last night," said Gorman, "but what he said is certainly not true." Union President McMahon also stated that Mr. Johnson is protecting capital. The mediation committee sent by President Roosevelt is still continuing its efforts to resolve the situation. However, both sides have made no concessions, so no progress has been made. of Evading $1 Million in Taxes 15

Mellon Expresses Astonishment Upon Hearing the News 16

(Washington) The US Treasury Department today filed another lawsuit against former Treasury Secretary Mellon for evading taxes on all income in 1931, alleging that he evaded over $1 million in taxes. It has requested the Tax Appeals Board to conduct a thorough investigation. Upon hearing the news, Mellon said that the Treasury Department's actions were extremely astonishing, attempting to re-litigate the old case that the Supreme Court had already ruled on in May in civil court. The Treasury Department's move is nothing more than an attempt to save face. It is reported that Mellon once served as the ambassador to the UK. In May of this year, he was accused by the Treasury Department of underpaying $1,319,000 in income tax in 1931, and the Treasury Department also requested the court to impose a fine of $659,540. At the time, Mellon said that the Treasury Department's case was the most contemptible political maneuver. In fact, he had paid the estimated income tax by the government. In the past 20 years, he had paid over $20 million in income tax. (Sixteenth Reuters Telegraph)

German Controlled Trade Policy 17

Central Government Establishes 25 Bureaus to Supervise Imports, Exports, Agriculture, Industry, and Commerce 18

Implemented from the 24th of This Month 19

Implemented from the 24th of this month. The authorities stated today that this regulation should not be interpreted as control. In order to protect foreign exporters from obtaining payment for their goods, the old system of allocating foreign currency to German importers will be changed. Therefore, importers will be notified in advance whether the Deutsche Bank is able to provide foreign currency to pay for imported goods. Therefore, the new system is actually a way to ensure that foreign exporters receive immediate payment for their goods. The authorities will now issue five orders regarding the transit of goods, the establishment of a raw materials control bureau, and changes to the laws on foreign currency control currently in force. From September 24th, Germany's import trade and industrial and agricultural commerce will be supervised by the 25 bureaus of the central government. (Fifteenth Reuters Telegraph)

(Berlin) Germany's foreign trade totaled 677,000,000 marks in August, a decrease of 7,000,000 marks compared to 684,000,000 marks in July. However, overall, there has actually been progress. The import surplus in August was only 9,000,000 marks, compared to 42,000,000 marks in July. With the exception of the 3,000,000 mark export surplus in March, August was actually the most profitable month for trade this year. This is clearly the result of controlled foreign trade. Taking imports as an example, the 363,000,000 marks in July decreased to 343,000,000 marks in August. The same month last year was 347,000,000 marks. Imports have decreased by 6% since July this year, mainly due to a decrease of 18,000,000 marks in food imports. The most optimistic aspect is that exports increased from 321,000,000 marks in July to 324,000,000 marks in August. The same month last year was 413,000,000 marks. Therefore, exports increased by 13,000,000 marks, or 4%, from July to August this year. The increase in imports was partly due to raw materials such as coal, and partly due to finished products, with roughly equal proportions. Exports to France, Switzerland, and the Netherlands decreased, but exports to Sweden, Italy, the UK, and Soviet Russia increased significantly, largely offsetting the decreases. (Fifteenth National Telegraph)

The Status of Women in Germany Under Hitler 20

The Doctrine of Good Wives and Mothers 21

(National News Agency German Correspondence) Dr. Wengel of Germany made the following remarks on the modern German woman. The content of German women's lives is to be sought in the family, so that they can gain a good reputation, be a housekeeper, or a good wife and mother. We firmly believe that this German plan will eventually be realized. A good mother is the highest ideal of modern German women. The meaning is not superficial, but specifically for the care of future children, for the sake of future human happiness. We know that children need to live in a healthy and happy family every day. It is the undeniable duty of mothers to manage children, and children must have a good family. We firmly believe that when parents share joys and sorrows and help each other, children will love their parents. In order to manage the family, women's bodies and spirits will naturally become stronger, so the feelings between families and couples will increase day by day, and wives, husbands, and children will feel more cheerful. Unmarried women should also enrich their lives and find spiritual comfort in life. Therefore, national socialism pays special attention to women's morality. Based on this principle, it rescues women, heals women, manages women, and supports women, so that female virtues do not decline, arouse women's interests, and work hard. Only in this way can we save the declining customs and realize women's happiness. As of now, there are many women in Germany who have received higher education, such as countless male and female college graduates, but most of these college students cannot adapt to the conditions of national life. Girls account for 10% of them. In essence, although female college students in Germany study at school, they are actually just listening to German lectures in college. Today, to solve the German women's problem, we cannot borrow from foreign countries. We must carefully observe the characteristics of Germany and not ignore Germany's long-standing customs, religion, and the status of German women. But we must observe the situation of German women in the past decade in order to understand everything. Modern German women are truly extremely happy. Our leader pays special attention to women's issues, but women must also be loyal to our party. In recent months, the German government has dealt with many issues concerning women, such as uniting many virtuous couples, enabling young and handsome men and women to form good relationships and live in peace. Secondly, if women from the age of 17 to 25 have to manage housework for up to 52 weeks, they will be able to reduce their taxes. Today, we cannot relax. If there are some women who cannot work for the country, we can advise them: think about it, we now need to build the country, we must follow the government's plan and implement it step by step. Men are the foundation of national construction, so women must basically be family attendants or managers in order to get through this very difficult period. We need strong women, married women manage housework, children, and serve their parents-in-law, and unmarried women cannot infringe on the status of men. We know very well that Germany is still in a difficult period, which is naturally the suffering of both men and women, but we must have a firm will to overcome this difficulty. In this way, there will definitely be a way out in the future.

Polish Bromberg German-Polish relations have indeed made considerable progress. One proof of this is that the regulations of the German Association organized in Poland have been formally approved by the Polish authorities. The purpose of this organization can be seen in one of the articles of the following organizational law: "The German Association is a united gathering of German-Polish people residing in the two provinces of Posen and Pomerania in Poland. In addition, there are also the editor's "Selected Current Affairs Commentaries," the reporter's "Bi-Monthly News Highlights," "Brief Records of Contemporary People's Words and Deeds," and "A Bundle of Miscellaneous News," etc. If everyone has a copy, not only will they have a clear understanding of the major events at home and abroad, but also they will be able to gain many insights in terms of personal cultivation. It is truly a valuable publication in the country. It is heard that the publication will extend the special price period to benefit readers, with a full-year subscription costing 50 cents domestically and 1 dollar and 50 cents abroad.

Medical News

Pingmin Obstetrics Hospital Vaccinates Against Smallpox: Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting, Wang Bozhuang, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Yuan Ludeng, Zhang Xiaolin, Gu Shaoqing, Wang Yanbin, Pan Gongzhan, and others, the founders of the Pingmin Obstetrics Hospital in Hongkou, Tilanqiao, are sparing no effort in providing facilities for the common people. In view of the autumn season's need to prevent smallpox, they have specially provided free smallpox vaccinations at the new hospital at No. 4 Tongzhou Road, No. 27 behind the Tilanqiao Police Station, and No. 32 Huade Road. On average, more than a hundred people are vaccinated every day. In addition to free deliveries, the hospital also has a nursery with many nannies dedicated to caring for newborns according to new childcare methods.

Calligraphy and Painting News

Xu Cifang's Calligraphy: Xu Cifang is the literary grandson of Xu Jihe, Vice Minister of the Ministry of Rites from Jiading, and the second son of Provincial Governor Xi Cheng of Jilin Province. He excels in poetry and prose and is skilled in regular script in the six styles of calligraphy, deeply inheriting the spirit of the Jin and Tang dynasties. His works are highly valued by renowned figures at home and abroad, but he is quite self-appreciative and does not always create for others. In recent years, he has been selling his calligraphy in Tianjin and Qingdao, and many friends have entrusted postal services to request his work from afar. Although Mr. Xu has reluctantly agreed, the round trips are delayed and costly. Now that Mr. Xu is residing in Shanghai for some matters, colleagues have requested that he make an exception for two months for those in this area who wish to request his calligraphy. He has agreed and has a discounted price list available. Please send letters requesting the list to Mr. Xu, No. 5 Mingde Lane, Huanlong Road, French Concession, this city.

Weather Report

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Around Shandong, the sky is clear and cloudy, with a gentle southeast wind. In the middle reaches of the Yangtze River, the sky is cloudy and overcast, and there may be showers in various places. The wind is coming from the southwest to the northwest. The area around here is cloudy, with thin fog in the morning and an uncertain wind direction. In the East China Sea, the wind is coming from the northeast to the southeast. The hurricane in the southeastern Pacific Ocean east of Luzon is currently stalling. Another hurricane southwest of the Ogasawara Islands is still heading northwest. The center of the first hurricane was within 120 miles of the intersection of 13 degrees north latitude and 133 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM yesterday, stalling or moving very slowly. The wind force is unknown. The center of the second hurricane was within 120 miles of the intersection of 17 degrees north latitude and 138 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM yesterday, heading northwest. The wind force is unknown. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 89.1 degrees and the lowest was 71.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 85.1 degrees and the lowest was 59.7 degrees.

Issue 27 Reading News

Compiled by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shenbao Circulation Library

Contents (1) Mailbox (2) Announcements

Mailbox (1) New Regulations for Individual Replies: Due to the daily increase in letters to this department, we previously answered letters from both those who had joined the "Reading Guidance" department and those who were only doing "Reading Q&A" indiscriminately. However, we now have to differentiate. We have temporarily decided that those who have joined the guidance department will have the right to receive replies earlier. We will still answer letters from general "Reading Q&A" readers as faithfully and as quickly as possible, without undue delay. As for the date of receiving replies, we will strictly implement the time that has already been announced in the previous issue (Issue 26).

(2) Reservation of Registration

This department has seen that many readers have registered with this department, but have not been seen discussing anything with us afterwards. Therefore, we feel that if they have no sincerity in reading, why bother with an empty name? Therefore, we have had to cancel the registration of some friends. Now, we have not received their letters stating whether they do not write because they are too busy with life to have time to read and write letters, or whether their boss deliberately interferes with their correspondence. Therefore, "I feel very ashamed, having not read, what is there to ask?" So I haven't been in touch for a long time, but they all requested that we still retain their registration. In their busy lives, they still want us to be able to "guide" them and have the opportunity to have a "life consultant." We are naturally willing to accept this request, but we hope that all readers in this situation will still use a few minutes of their spare time to write us a few words each month to notify us. We not only welcome such diligent readers to communicate, but also welcome such friends to talk (however, please make an appointment in advance).

(3) No Reply for Unclear Addresses

We will not reply to any submissions that do not include a mailing address. In the future, we will only publish names in this publication for those who cannot send mail this week: Shen Jing, Liu Fang, He Menghu. Announcements

Today's Reading Q&A is suspended for one day. Tomorrow's Reading Q&A will continue to publish "Attitude Towards Work." Please pay special attention to this reply.

Spring and Autumn

Little West Heaven

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 2 Sold into the Homes of Ordinary People, Returning to Yongshou, Leaving Home, Heavenly People Arrive in Chang'an

Zhang Jiefu first felt that his words were somewhat inappropriate, so he said: "What I mean is, seeing the people suffering so much here, what are your thoughts?" Li Shilian said: "As the saying goes, 'The people's feelings are like iron, the law of the officials is like a furnace; there is no soybean in the world that cannot be squeezed for oil.' I didn't quite believe these words before, but now I understand." The section chief, hearing him talk on and on, always about the affairs inside the tax collection agency, laughed and said: "Mr. Li has always been in charge of taxation, right? It can truly be said that three sentences cannot leave the profession." Only then did Li Shilian realize that he had been careless in his speech and had been seen through. His face flushed for a moment, and he forced a smile, not daring to say anything more. With this little anecdote, it was inconvenient to discuss this dilapidated manor any further. The driver had finished adding water and repaired the car. Everyone got in and continued driving forward. For those who had never been here before, everyone couldn't help but think that King Wen of Zhou built the road more than 2,000 years ago. Logically, the trees here should be denser than those of the Han and Tang dynasties. Furthermore, such a great emperor's tomb must also be in a place with beautiful mountains and rivers. Everyone eagerly looked out of the car, wanting to be the first to see the ancient relics. Unexpectedly, the car drove onto a plateau, and under the broad daylight, all that could be seen was a vast expanse of yellow earth, gradually rising until it met the sky in the distance. In the middle of this, there were some mounds as high as houses, either standing alone or clustered together in groups of three or five, obviously man-made, but no one could guess what they were for. Zhang Jiefu said: "Are these tombs? Why are they so big?" Li Shilian had already misspoke himself and did not dare to answer, fearing that he would make another joke. The other two people in the car seemed to have formed their own group. They only looked at Zhang and Li, as if with a smile on their faces (20).

Supplement of Old Newspapers 26

— By Liu Cunren

I have a very special hobby in my life, which is to collect newspapers from various places. Now, gathered together, I already have more than a hundred kinds. Sometimes there are many valuable historical materials inside that cannot be found elsewhere.

I have a Shimin Daily from the Guangxu period of the late Qing Dynasty. The content is extremely simple. There is a lack of political and social news, only government reports, announcements, imperial records, etc.; but the supplement is very rich: there are new jokes, and the Guangya New Bishi novel written by Shi Nanchu. Reading it now, I really feel a different flavor. Let me cite an extraordinary omen as follows: "In the Xinhai year of the first year of Xianfeng (1851), the Chu Bei provincial examination had the topic of 'When the world is righteous, ordinary people do not criticize.' A certain top scholar, when explaining the last sentence, said: 'It feels like a scene of peace is right before our eyes.' At that time, Hunan was warning of danger. A year later, Chu Bei fell, and the words 'Taiping Heavenly Kingdom' were everywhere on notices, door plaques, and flags. This student deliberately made a good omen to please the times, but unexpectedly it became a prophecy." Isn't this good material for a Red Sheep Heroic Biography?

Speaking of newspapers in the interior, none of the dozens of kinds that I have retained are perfect. The layout of the Henan Evening News is very good, the structure of the Beijing Evening News is very new, and the editorials of the Jiangxi Raozhou Minbao are very proper. These are their special strengths. The most complete newspaper promoting vernacular Chinese is the Beiping Vernacular Real Report, which uses all new-style punctuation.

The content of Guangzhou newspapers need not be mentioned for now, but the supplements can be considered extremely bad: they are all diary-style shoddy things. Comparatively speaking, the Republican Daily is more well-known. But it's still not as good as newspapers from other places.

As for Tianjin, Beiping, Jinan, Nanjing...etc., I cannot talk about them all at once. I didn't expect that collecting small newspaper supplements would fill a large belly of history!

Red Paper Packet 28

— Spring Rain Building Master

The wonderful use of red paper packets is very broad, and they contain a mysterious meaning. For example, when asking a Chinese medicine doctor to diagnose an illness, after opening the prescription, you have to take out a red paper packet from your side, which is considered the consultation fee, the amount ranging from several dimes to several yuan. However, the polite doctors need to decline with you for a while, and never count the amount inside the packet in person. This shows the profound mystery of the red paper packet.

There is another thing that makes me confused. Since I was a child, I suffered from malaria every day. The onset was very fierce. After a few days, my face was yellow and thin, and I had no appetite. My parents were very worried, but they didn't know about swallowing quinine. They specialized in getting some small secret prescriptions, or asked someone to draw a talisman on a cake to eat in the morning facing the sun. Or they asked someone to send the malaria ghost out of the house, but none of them worked. One day, my mother used a small square of red paper and wrapped seven grains of raw rice, seven tea leaves, and a Shunzhi copper coin inside. She placed it by my side. My mother accompanied me out for a walk. When we reached the crossroads, she secretly threw away the red paper packet, without looking back. I did the same, and sure enough, the malaria did not come that day.

A certain woman in Huzhou engaged in prostitution, but she also had to consider her husband's face, so she came up with a method of using a red paper packet. The method was to put a red paper packet at the door, implying that there was someone inside, and the husband would not enter. If there was no red paper packet at the door, it meant that there were no guests inside. This was indeed a very clever hint.

The Function of the Alliance 29

— Shiying

The Cow Butcher 30

— Shen Shouruo

Because of the restoration of the old ritual of worshipping Confucius, I was reminded of the cow butcher.

In the former Qing Dynasty, Confucius was worshipped twice a year, in spring and autumn. The most important sacrificial offering was the cow, called the "tailao" (great offering). The government paid the money, the rites department handled it, and the cow butcher procured it. And there were many interesting malpractices in between!

For example, if the government allocated 30 yuan to the rites department for the price of the cow, then the more kindhearted rites department would at least skim off 10 yuan, and the more ruthless ones would naturally take half, or even more, and then pass it on to the cow butcher for procurement.

The position of cow butcher was bestowed by the official government. Of course, he had to be on duty for procuring the tailao for worshipping Confucius, but it wasn't a business if he had to pay for it himself. The axe eats the chisel, and the chisel eats the wood, so of course he had a place to eat from as well.

The cow heads (that is, the brokers who buy and sell cattle) in each village had a customary practice of buying the cow butcher's account. Therefore, the cow butcher not only charged them illegal fees every year, but also ordered them to supply the tailao. If they didn't buy his account, then! Then! Sorry, just issue a ticket on some pretext, and the guest ticket would come. Therefore, the cow heads had to buy his account, which was an unspeakable grievance!

At the same time, the cow butcher was necessarily the executioner. He handled both killing cows and killing people, and he can be said to be the number one slaughter machine for both humans and animals. So his attitude, which I still dread, was very imposing, fierce, and terrifying!

Small Recipe

御香縹緲錄 31

— Written by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

He pretended to be extremely loyal, saying that he was acting on a secret edict from Emperor Guangxu to assassinate the Empress Dowager, but upon reflection, he couldn't bear to do it. Therefore, he defied Guangxu's orders and came to inform on him. Although his words were so empty and without any real evidence, the Empress Dowager completely trusted him. So that very night, he led the troops he had brought and escorted the Empress Dowager, using a lightning-fast method, straight into Guangxu's bedroom. The Empress Dowager was in a great rage at this time and, disregarding all decorum, ordered people to drag Guangxu out of bed. Without even asking a question, she immediately forced him to sign an edict ceding power back to her. The result of this life-or-death struggle was that the Empress Dowager regained control and resumed her former power, while Guangxu was greatly unlucky! From then on, the Empress Dowager vowed never to forgive him, ignoring everything he said. Of course, Guangxu was sure to bear a bitter grudge against Yuan Shikai for this betrayal and deeply resent it, but unfortunately, he never got to avenge himself! When he followed the Empress Dowager on this yellow train to Tianjin, he had already spent six or seven years of the political prisoner's life Yuan Shikai had bestowed upon him. In fact, he never regained his freedom until his death.

Now, let's see! This prisoner-like Emperor Guangxu is approaching his enemy! Although he is riding in another carriage, so many officials have come to greet them at the station. How could he hide and not come out? He must stand respectfully behind the Empress Dowager, accepting the greetings of these people. I remember that whenever the Empress Dowager was not around, when Guangxu and I were casually talking, I often heard him talk about his feelings about the Hundred Days' Reform. Every time, he would gnash his teeth and curse Yuan Shikai, who fabricated lies and framed him. So I had long held an extremely excited heart, planning to see his expression after meeting Yuan Shikai face to face. (129)

Sports News

American Baseball Team Scheduled to Arrive in Shanghai

A Team of Sixteen Arrives on December 4th

Baseball King Babe Ruth is Also Among Them

All of Them are World-Class American Players

The American baseball team, a group of sixteen, including baseball king Babe Ruth, are all world-class American professional baseball players. They will participate in this year's World Series and will form a team to travel to East Asia in October. They are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on December 4th. The local Western baseball teams have all heard the news and are very excited. The details are as follows:

Tour Itinerary The team is scheduled to depart from Vancouver on the Changxing Steamer on October 22nd. They will have three games in Honolulu and then go to Japan. They will stay in Japan for a month and will have as many as sixteen exhibition games. Then, on December 2nd, they will leave Kobe for Shanghai and are scheduled to arrive on the 4th. They will leave Shanghai for Manila on the 5th and have six or seven games in the Philippines. Therefore, they will only stay in Shanghai for one day.

Performance in Shanghai The Shanghai Amateur Baseball Association, upon hearing the news, immediately telegraphed Mr. Heibe, the manager of the team in Philadelphia, asking the team to give an exhibition game when they arrive in Shanghai, competing against a mixed team of the Shanghai Mais and Japanese teams. However, they have not yet received a reply from Philadelphia. December 4th is when the weather in Shanghai is severely cold. Whether the team is willing to perform in the cold is still a question. The reason why the team cannot come to the East earlier is that they must wait until after the World Series finals before they can leave the United States.

The Hongkou Cross-Country Team held its 56th cross-country running general practice yesterday at 4:30 pm, starting from the west gate of Hongkou Park, passing through Jiangwan Road and turning into East Sports Road, running along Xiangyin Road across the Jiangwan Racecourse, and returning to the original location. Liang Yaoting and Zhang Jincai led the way, with Chen Ribin and Xu Houze closely following behind.
